+0000","feedId":591,"bgimg":"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/YT_Thumbnail_Build_2880x1200_rev1.max-1300x1300.png","linkMd5":"9eec5130baecb9a8b7bb026da778d7c7","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn65@2020_6/2020/08/16/12-13-03-536_f9bd52e98b1533dd.webp","metaImg":"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/YT_Thumbnail_Build_2880x1200_rev1.max-1300x1300.png","destWidth":1300,"destHeight":541,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx17/cdn10@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-00-698_4bbeb52263385580.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?i=nGIj9ZXu4iA:XaHp9AfYgQA:-BTjWOF_DHI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn85@2020_5/2020/08/16/12-12-00-575_4c53a946441ee694.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/blogspot/SbSV/~4/nGIj9ZXu4iA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx17/cdn66@2020_1/2020/08/16/12-12-03-204_e2b00d2c9847016d.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","title":"Connecting people to virtual care options","link":"https://blog.google/technology/health/virtual-care-covid-19/","description":"<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <br />\n  <p>To prevent the spread of COVID-19, many healthcare providers are reducing or stopping in-person visits for a variety of patient needs, from the treatment of chronic conditions to mental health services to evaluating cough and cold symptoms. Yet, people need a way to continue getting medical care from the comfort and safety of their own homes. Since the beginning of the pandemic, we’ve seen interest in virtual care and telehealth <a href=\"https://trends.google.com/trends/explore?geo=US&amp;q=telehealth\">rise dramatically</a>. Health consultations over the phone or by video conference not only help alleviate strain on doctors’ offices and emergency rooms but are also recommended as an important way to <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/hcp/preparedness-resources.html\">protect patients and staff</a> against COVID-19.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>To help individuals and health care providers connect, we’re focused on providing individuals with access to high-quality and <a href=\"https://www.blog.google/products/search/connecting-people-covid-19-information-and-resources/\">authoritative information</a> and supporting them throughout their health journey. Over the coming week, we’re beginning to roll out two new features in Search and Maps that make it easier for people to connect to virtual healthcare options, whether it’s to a doctor’s office down the street, the hospital across town, or a national telehealth platform.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>Local healthcare providers, now virtual</h3>\n  <p>Healthcare providers like hospitals, doctors, and mental health professionals can now enter a virtual care offering in their Business Profile, so that people searching for their local provider, for instance, might see a “get online care” link on Search and Maps. Clicking this link will take people to that provider’s virtual care website where they can find more information, and in many cases, schedule a virtual healthcare visit with a provider.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>The pandemic has affected many healthcare providers’ operating hours and walk-in visit policies. To help communicate changes that might affect someone’s visit, we’re automatically surfacing a link directly to health providers’ COVID-19 information page on Search and Maps, and we've assembled <a href=\"https://support.google.com/webmasters/answer/9781983\">best practices</a> on how healthcare providers can update their websites and provide <a href=\"https://support.google.com/business/?p=covid_posts\">COVID-19</a> information on <a href=\"https://support.google.com/business/answer/9798848?hl=en&amp;ref_topic=4539639\">Google My Business</a>.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 \">\n    <img alt=\"New health information about Hillview Hospital\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/hospital.max-1000x1000.jpg\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>With health providers limiting in-person visits due to COVID-19, we’re making it easier for people to discover virtual care options.</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>Find virtual healthcare, anywhere, anytime</h3>\n  <p>Beginning as a pilot in the U.S., we’ll also begin showing widely-available virtual care platforms directly on Search so people can more easily access virtual visits. For example, when people search for “immediate care”, we’ll be able to also present available virtual care options and related information such as the out-of-pocket price charged for a visit (for those without insurance) and an easy way for people to directly connect with the virtual care platform. The visit between the patient and provider will take place on the healthcare provider’s platform of choice.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 \">\n    <img alt=\"On Search, you can see information about virtual healthcare platforms\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/virtual_Care_2_CoIc1II.gif\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>People will be able to see&nbsp;widely-available virtual healthcare platforms&nbsp;directly on Search as well as the out-of-pocket cost for a visit.</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>For healthcare providers, helping you keep up with demand</h3>\n  <p>In addition to helping healthcare providers with information about how to keep their online <a href=\"https://support.google.com/business/answer/9798848?hl=en&amp;ref_topic=4539639\">business information up-to-date</a>, Google Cloud is supporting <a href=\"https://cloud.google.com/covid19-healthcare\">providers with technology infrastructure and solutions</a> to assist with care delivery and operations. This includes helping doctors support patients remotely with <a href=\"https://support.google.com/a/answer/3407054?hl=en\">HIPAA-compliant</a> G Suite products (including using Google Meet for telehealth or virtual visits),<a href=\"https://cloud.google.com/solutions/contact-center/covid19-rapid-response\">deploying virtual agents</a> to field questions related to COVID-19, and helping with capacity-planning and demand forecasting of key medical supplies to better manage their supply chains.</p>\n  <p>The global COVID-19 pandemic and the response to prevent its spread has changed the way individuals access and connect to health care. Across our products, we’ll continue to ensure that healthcare providers have the tools to connect with patients, and that anyone can access the information and care they need to stay healthy.</p>\n </div>\n</div>","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Fri, 10 Apr 2020 15:00:00 +0000","feedId":591,"bgimg":"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/hospital.max-1000x1000.jpg","linkMd5":"dd7467931a5d99c29a38724ae30deaa1","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn13@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-11-59-760_e267d3ecbd7ec491.webp","destWidth":800,"destHeight":800,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/hospital.max-1000x1000.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn22@2020_3/2020/08/16/12-11-59-825_e267d3ecbd7ec491.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/virtual_Care_2_CoIc1II.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn73@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-09-581_6db42458b40399ac.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx17/cdn10@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-00-698_4bbeb52263385580.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?i=PdzNh78UrBo:Tmej6zuG13U:-BTjWOF_DHI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn82@2020_3/2020/08/16/12-12-01-802_9eda9707e63e709b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/blogspot/SbSV/~4/PdzNh78UrBo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn69@2020_3/2020/08/16/12-12-01-689_7c7b2579cd2902a6.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","title":"Get around safely with these new Google Maps features","link":"https://blog.google/products/maps/get-around-safely-these-new-google-maps-features/","description":"<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>Getting from A to B can be more complicated these days. Because of COVID-19, it’s increasingly important to know how crowded a train station might be at a particular time or whether the bus is running on a limited schedule. Having this information before and during your trip is critical for both essential workers who need to safely navigate to work and will become more important for everyone as countries around the world begin to reopen.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>In our latest release of Google Maps on Android and iOS, we’re introducing features to help you easily find important information if you need to venture out, whether it’s by car or public transportation.&nbsp;</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>Get alerts about important information&nbsp;</h3>\n  <p>When you look up public transit directions for a trip that is likely to be affected by COVID-19 restrictions, we’ll show relevant alerts from local transit agencies. These alerts can help you prepare accordingly if government mandates impact transit services or require you to wear a mask on public transportation. Transit alerts are rolling out in Argentina, Australia, Belgium, Brazil, Colombia, France, India, Mexico, Netherlands, Spain, Thailand, United Kingdom and the U.S. where we have information from local transit agencies, with more coming soon.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>We’re also introducing driving alerts to notify you about COVID-19 checkpoints and restrictions along your route, like when crossing national borders (starting first in Canada, Mexico and the U.S.). You’ll see an alert on the directions screen and after starting navigation if your route is impacted by these restrictions.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>When navigating to medical facilities or COVID-19 testing centers, we’ll display an alert reminding you to verify eligibility and facility guidelines to avoid being turned away or causing additional strain on the local healthcare system. Starting this week, alerts for medical facilities will be available in Indonesia, Israel, the Philippines, South Korea, and the U.S., and testing center alerts will be available in the U.S.</p>\n dot click&quot;\n           }\"></div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>We’re showing these alerts where we’ve received authoritative data from local, state and federal governments or from their websites, and are actively working with other agencies around the world to bring even more of this helpful data to users in Google Maps. Interested agencies can get in touch <a href=\"https://support.google.com/mapcontentpartners/answer/9359574?hl=en\">here</a> for driving restrictions and <a href=\"https://support.google.com/transitpartners/#topic=3521043\">here</a> for transit alerts.&nbsp;</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>Safely avoid crowds on public transit&nbsp;</h3>\n  <p>Last year, we&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.blog.google/products/maps/grab-seat-and-be-time-new-transit-updates-google-maps/\">introduced</a>&nbsp;crowdedness predictions for public transit in Google Maps. Powered by tens of millions of contributions from past riders, these predictions help people see how crowded a particular bus line or train tends to be. We’re now making it simpler for people to contribute crowdedness information for their transit lines. Look up Directions, tap through to see the Transit Details, then scroll down to find crowdedness predictions (where available) and easily contribute your own experiences.</p>\n  <p>Additionally, in February, we&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.blog.google/products/maps/maps-15th-birthday/\">announced</a>&nbsp;new insights like temperature, accessibility and security onboard, as well as designated women’s sections in regions where transit systems have them. These insights are now rolled out globally, helping you find feedback from past riders when available and submit your own, right alongside public transit routes. To help wheelchair users around the world know before they go, we’ve added more granular accessibility information for people to find and contribute, including where there are wheelchair accessible doors, seating, stop buttons and more.&nbsp;</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--medium h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--4 h-c-grid__col--offset-4 \">\n    <img alt=\"crowdedness-10.43.gif\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/crowdedness-10.43.gif\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>Find and contribute crowdedness information for transit lines.&nbsp;</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>To ensure proper social distancing, commuters are paying attention to how crowded or comfortable their ride and transit station will be. Starting today, you can easily see the times when a transit station is historically more or less busy to plan your trip accordingly or you can look at live data showing how busy it is right now compared to its usual level of activity. Simply search for a station in Google Maps or tap on the station on the map to see the departure board and busyness data, where available. Rolling out over the next several weeks, these capabilities are powered by aggregated and anonymized data from users who have opted in to Google Location History, a Google account-level setting that is off by default. To protect privacy, these insights are only surfaced when we have sufficient data to meet privacy thresholds.&nbsp;</p>\n  <br />\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--medium h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--4 h-c-grid__col--offset-4 \">\n    <img alt=\"busyness-10.43.gif\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/busyness-10.43.gif\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>See popular times for a transit station and how busy it is at that moment.</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>COVID-19 has certainly impacted the way that we move around in the world. As cities and countries across the globe adapt, we’re committed to bringing the most pertinent information right to your fingertips. So when you’re ready and able to, you can safely venture out.</p>\n  <br />\n </div>\n</div>","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Mon, 08 Jun 2020 15:00:00 +0000","feedId":591,"bgimg":"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/crowdedness-10.43.gif","linkMd5":"0eb62c8047ca6e70093c740220dbd4a5","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn26@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-20-012_bdf8005af93d2e17.webp","destWidth":550,"destHeight":1053,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/crowdedness-10.43.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn50@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-27-638_bdf8005af93d2e17.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/busyness-10.43.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn6@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-22-056_fb66f9b04d25db46.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx17/cdn10@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-00-698_4bbeb52263385580.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?i=WvIqB72ETV4:mN8NQ4lWtsY:-BTjWOF_DHI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn65@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-01-695_2b6b18c4aa5a102a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/blogspot/SbSV/~4/WvIqB72ETV4":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx20/cdn94@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-11-59-562_61f9482e08c5f941.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","title":"Essential Google Maps tricks for your next road trip","link":"https://blog.google/products/maps/google-maps-summer-road-trip-tips/","description":"<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>Scroll through Denise Barlock’s public <a href=\"https://www.google.com/maps/contrib/106543964909796395027\">Google Maps profile</a> and you’ll notice one thing: Denise is always on the road and she leaves a trail of reviews and photos in her wake. As of today, Denise has posted more than 1,000 reviews across 35 states and two countries. Along the way, she has shared over 12,000 photos from places like restaurants, grocery stores, and campsites, which have been viewed roughly 95 million times</p>\n  <p>Four years ago, Denise retired early and bought an Entegra Class A motorhome that she named “Maggie.” She now calls the entire United States her home. Since transforming her retirement into a country-trotting journey, Denise has traveled 54,000 miles across the U.S. and has driven as far north as Alaska. A Google Maps superuser and Level 10&nbsp;<a href=\"https://maps.google.com/localguides\">Local Guide</a>, she has collected helpful tips for others: go&nbsp;<a href=\"https://youtu.be/17XKU7k2zcA\">off-roading</a>&nbsp;in the Southwest during the winter; visit&nbsp;<a href=\"https://youtu.be/odS7eUmyW74\">Colorado&nbsp;</a>to see the aspens change color in the fall; stay overnight at an&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.google.com/maps/place/Blue+Mesa+Alpacas/@35.5134883,-105.90569,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m5!3m4!1s0x8718f8e620c3b78d:0xb8f2ef1e12b0672d!8m2!3d35.5134883!4d-105.9035013\">alpaca farm</a>&nbsp;in Santa Fe, New Mexico; and search for the decorative&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IxvPz839qfA\">flamingo</a>&nbsp;you’re bound to find somewhere on the premises of almost every RV park.</p>\n  <p>Traveling more than 12,000 miles a year and changing her location about once a month, Denise has come to know Google Maps inside and out. And with many Americans taking to the road this summer, she graciously offered to share essential tips on how to maximize Google Maps to make your next road trip more enjoyable, memorable, budget-friendly and stress-free.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>Whether you’re hauling your family on a cross-country RV trip or going for a scenic day trip, Denise’s six Google Maps road trip tips are not to miss.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_carousel\">\n <div class=\"h-c-page article-module\">\n  <div class=\"article-module glue-pagination h-c-carousel h-c-carousel--simple class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Search for food\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Search_for_food_2J5di8J.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <p><b>1.&nbsp;Eat like a local: Find restaurants and businesses en route</b></p>Part of experiencing a new place is trying the local cuisine. Use Google Maps to search for restaurants within the $ and $$ range, and you’ll usually find the more frequently visited local restaurants. Scan the reviews to find out what’s frequently talked about, like the can’t-miss&nbsp;chicken fried steak in Carthage, Texas, or an amazing hatch chili burger in New Mexico. Google Maps will even tell you what dishes are most popular based on the reviews and photos other diners have left behind.\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Explore tab\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Explore_tab_n1E9nsg.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <b>2. Explore more: Maximize the Google Maps search bar and Explore tab</b>\n     <p>Find interesting places and things to do with Google Maps. Use the search bar in Google Maps to look for specific things like “scenic spots,” “waterfall,” or “trailhead.” Try using more detailed searches to get better results when looking for a business or service. For example, search for “oceanfront RV campground,” “early bird specials,” or “kayak rental daily rate.”</p>\n     <p><br /></p>\n     <p></p>\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Takeout and delivery\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Takeout_and_delivery_2.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <b>3. Plan ahead: Look for restaurants doing takeout, dine-in or delivery</b>\n     <p>COVID-19 has forced many restaurants to change their operating models or even temporarily close, which makes planning ahead even more important. With Google Maps you can look for local restaurants around you that are open, offering takeout, curbside pickup, delivery or no-contact delivery.</p>\n     <p><br /></p>\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Search Gas Stations\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Search_Gas_Stations.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <b>4. Save on the go: Cut back on gas and toll money&nbsp;</b>\n     <p>Expenses can add up quickly when you’re on the road. If you need to make a pit stop, you can use Google Maps to search for nearby gas stations and their prices to get the best deal. This is especially helpful in places like the Colorado mountains where gas stations are limited and you need to make sure you have a full tank at the best price before driving over mountain passes.&nbsp;</p>\n     <p>You can also avoid toll roads and highways when in navigation mode. Given the price of tolls for big rigs in the Northeast and across the country, Denise tries to avoid the toll roads as much as possible. As you’re viewing your directions, simply tap on the three dots at the top right corner of the Google Maps to see your route options and select the route types you want to avoid.</p>\n     <p></p>\n     <p><br /></p>\n     <p></p>\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Save a Place\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Save_a_Place.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <b>5. Keep track: Save the places you’ve been and the places you want to go</b>\n     <p>Use the nifty Saved tab to create custom lists of favorite places you’ve been and places you want to visit and even share your lists with others.&nbsp;</p>\n     <p>Open the Google Maps app and find that must-try BBQ spot that you’ve planned a day trip around. Tap on the place name and then the “Save” icon to add the place to one of several pre-set lists like “Want to Go” or “Favorites.” You can also add places to a new list that you name yourself, like “Finger Lickin’ BBQ.” Use the Saved tab to find lists you’ve created and followed.&nbsp;</p>\n     <p>Denise has a custom list of places she considers to be “best-of” in the Surfside Beach area of <a href=\"https://www.google.com/maps/@/data=!3m1!4b1!4m3!11m2!2sbYpYDWi_Fs6AXXN7eZPepCGk3sKveQ!3e3?shorturl=1\">Myrtle Beach, SC</a>. She will oftentimes create private lists that consist of local vets, drug stores, and grocery stores to be able to find these needed services quickly and easily.</p>\n     <p></p>\n     <p><br /></p>\n     <p></p>\n     <p></p>\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph_with_image\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap\">\n   <div class=\"uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3\" data-component=\"uni-article-paragraph\">\n    <figure class=\"article-image--wrap-medium \">\n     <img alt=\"Leave a review\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Leave_a_review.gif\" />\n    </figure>\n    <div class=\"rich-text\">\n     <b>6. Pay it forward: Leave reviews and share photos</b>\n     <p>Other travelers took the time to leave the Google Maps reviews and photos that helped you make a decision on your road trip. Pay it forward to the next road warrior and leave your own reviews and photos of the places that made your visit memorable. Doing so also gives small businesses exposure to other travelers, and makes them more likely to be around the next time you roll through town.<br /></p>\n     <p></p>\n     <p><br /></p>\n +0000","feedId":591,"bgimg":"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Search_for_food_2J5di8J.gif","linkMd5":"e70c2a51115caa927bf324dd2c6171c7","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx20/cdn46@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-08-383_5cf449a03e1bf938.webp","destWidth":1000,"destHeight":1000,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Search_for_food_2J5di8J.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn42@2020_6/2020/08/16/12-12-13-718_5cf449a03e1bf938.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Explore_tab_n1E9nsg.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn33@2020_6/2020/08/16/12-12-17-879_b54e8434abf7a3b7.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Takeout_and_delivery_2.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn62@2020_5/2020/08/16/12-12-09-115_ba1cfe39c908e4e2.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Search_Gas_Stations.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn97@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-16-969_5081c0eea1231be6.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Save_a_Place.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn41@2020_3/2020/08/16/12-12-08-803_c9239d09feaf2f18.webp","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Leave_a_review.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn26@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-12-12-391_30ca1209e473fbd5.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx17/cdn10@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-12-00-698_4bbeb52263385580.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/blogspot/SbSV?i=6yJFB62dzu8:mR1Os6wYOgk:-BTjWOF_DHI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn49@2020_1/2020/08/16/12-12-00-508_b582acda313ae8eb.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/blogspot/SbSV/~4/6yJFB62dzu8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn54@2020_1/2020/08/16/12-11-59-573_b0c54a16076baf10.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:11:59","title":"Helping public health officials combat COVID-19","link":"https://blog.google/technology/health/covid-19-community-mobility-reports/","description":"<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>As global communities respond to the COVID-19 pandemic, there has been an increasing emphasis on public health strategies, like social distancing measures, to slow the rate of transmission. In Google Maps, we <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XIvn02V2U8o\">use</a> aggregated, anonymized data showing how busy certain types of places are—helping identify when a local business tends to be the most crowded. We have heard from public health officials that this same type of aggregated, anonymized data could be helpful as they make critical decisions to combat COVID-19.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>Starting today we’re publishing an early release of our <a href=\"http://google.com/covid19/mobility\">COVID-19 Community Mobility Reports</a> to provide insights into what has changed in response to work from home, shelter in place, and other policies aimed at flattening the curve of this pandemic. These reports have been developed to be helpful while adhering to our stringent privacy protocols and <a href=\"https://policies.google.com/privacy\">policies</a>.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>The reports use aggregated, anonymized data to chart movement trends over time by geography, across different high-level categories of places such as retail and recreation, groceries and pharmacies, parks, transit stations, workplaces, and residential. We’ll show trends over several weeks, with the most recent information representing 48-to-72 hours prior. While we display a percentage point increase or decrease in visits, we do not share the absolute number of visits. To protect people’s privacy, no personally identifiable information, like an individual’s location, contacts or movement, is made available at any point.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>We will release these reports globally, initially covering 131 countries and regions. Given the urgent need for this information, where possible we will also provide insights at the regional level. In the coming weeks, we will work to add additional countries and regions to ensure these reports remain helpful to public health officials across the globe looking to protect people from the spread of COVID-19.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 \">\n    <img alt=\"Global_Blogpost_Search_Spain.gif\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/original_images/Global_Blogpost_Search_Spain.gif\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>Navigate and download a report for your region of interest</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>In addition to other resources public health officials might have, we hope these reports will help support decisions about how to manage the COVID-19 pandemic. For example, this information could help officials understand changes in essential trips that can shape recommendations on business hours or inform delivery service offerings. Similarly, persistent visits to transportation hubs might indicate the need to add additional buses or trains in order to allow people who need to travel room to spread out for social distancing. Ultimately, understanding not only whether people are traveling, but also trends in destinations, can help officials design guidance to protect public health and essential needs of communities.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-image_full_width\">\n <div class=\"article-module h-c-page\">\n  <div class=\"h-c-grid\">\n   <figure class=\"article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 \">\n    <img alt=\"Global_Blogpost_LA_Report_zoom.png\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/Global_Blogpost_LA_Report_zoom.max-1000x1000.png\" />\n    <figcaption class=\"article-image__caption \">\n     <div class=\"rich-text\">\n      <p>A Community Mobility Report example for State of Louisiana, United States</p>\n     </div>\n    </figcaption>\n   </figure>\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <p>In addition to the Community Mobility Reports, we are collaborating with select epidemiologists working on COVID-19 with updates to an existing aggregate, anonymized <a href=\"https://ai.googleblog.com/2019/11/new-insights-into-human-mobility-with.html\">dataset</a> that can be used to better understand and forecast the pandemic. Data of this type has helped researchers look into <a href=\"https://journals.plos.org/plospathogens/article?id=10.1371/journal.ppat.1003932\">predicting epidemics</a>, plan urban and transit <a href=\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/29320477\">infrastructure</a>, and understand people’s <a href=\"https://www.nature.com/articles/s41467-019-12809-y\">mobility</a> and responses to conflict and <a href=\"https://www.pnas.org/content/109/29/11576\">natural disasters</a>.</p>\n </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"block-paragraph\">\n <div class=\"rich-text\">\n  <h3>Privacy protections</h3>\n  <p>The Community Mobility Reports are powered by the same world-class anonymization technology that we use in our products every day. For these reports, we use <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FfAdemDkLsc&amp;feature=youtu.be\">differential privacy</a>, which adds artificial noise to our datasets enabling high quality results without identifying any individual person.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>The insights are created with aggregated, anonymized sets of data from users who have turned on the <a href=\"https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/3118687?hl=en\">Location History</a> setting, which is off by default. Users who have Location History turned on can choose to turn the setting off at any time from their <a href=\"https://myaccount.google.com/activitycontrols\">Google Account</a>, and can always delete Location History data directly from their <a href=\"https://www.google.com/maps/timeline\">Timeline</a>.&nbsp;</p>\n  <p>These are unprecedented times and we will continue to evaluate these reports as we get feedback from public health officials, civil society groups, local governments and the community at large. We hope these insights will add to other public health information that will help people and communities stay healthy and safe.</p>\n
